style="border: 0px;" width="495" /></a></div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div style="text-align: justify;"><sup class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-reference"><br class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-reference">An&nbsp;<strong>anachronism</strong>&nbsp;(from the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719729000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHDOp_IuxqsSvCQI2iblRdPATSvfA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" style="color: #1155cc;" target="_blank" title="Ancient Greek">Greek</a>&nbsp;ἀνά&nbsp;<em>ana</em>, "against" and χρόνος&nbsp;<em>khronos</em>, "time") is a&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chronology&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719730000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGJREcUsAhmV_NwsZk-fW2aybeHbA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chronology" style="color: #1155cc;" target="_blank" title="Chronology">chronological</a>&nbsp;inconsistency in some arrangement, especially a juxtaposition of persons, events, objects, or customs from different periods of time. The most common type of anachronism is an object misplaced in time, but it may be a verbal expression, a technology, a philosophical idea, a musical style, a material, a plant or animal, a custom or anything else associated with a particular period in time so that it is incorrect to place it outside its proper temporal domain.</sup></div></div><div><br /></div><div><img alt="Inline image 18" height="68" src="reqs/fromthemachine.org/irmax_files/saved_resource(27)" style="border: 0px; data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3Dce76595b-6287-46f9-90b5-4cd9328ec0dd%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719736000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGhf-lXpf4Jzcyg5HWjdjPdsrS2Dw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Heinrich_der_Gl%C3%AEchez%C3%A6re" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Heinrich der Glîchezære">Heinrich der Glîchezære</a>. The 13th-century Heidelberg manuscript reads in part, "ouch hoer ich sagen, das sippe blůt von wazzere niht verdirbet" (lines 265-266). In English we read, "I also hear it said, kin-blood is not spoiled by water."</span><br /><span style="font-size: xx-small;"><br /></span><br /><div><span style="font-size: xx-small;">Authors Albert Jack<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-cite_ref-5" style="font-size: 6.75px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline;"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D84daa5da-1da5-49a0-bebf-c93f3a82c1c2%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719736000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFNDexZB3XGqV2og_3aSrkfqeAXyQ" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blood_is_thicker_than_water#cite_note-5" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank">[5]</a></span>&nbsp;and R. Richard Pustelniak<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-cite_ref-Pustelniak_6-0" style="font-size: 6.75px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline;"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3Df17298c2-9a4f-4abf-a806-d58c47258515%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719736000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFS1lRuYI1UG3M8gR_qbPD1_qdgzA" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blood_is_thicker_than_water#cite_note-Pustelniak-6" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank">[6]</a></span>&nbsp;claim the original meaning of the expression was that the ties between people who've made a blood covenant were stronger than ties formed by "the water of the womb". However, no known historical sources predating the modern era contain the blood-covenant version of the expression.</span><br /><span style="font-size: xx-small;"><br /></span><span style="font-size: xx-small;">The use of the word "blood" to refer to kin or familial relations has roots dating back to Greek and Roman traditions.<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-cite_ref-7" style="font-size: 6.75px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline;"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D1f7fec60-d707-4624-8000-d2d90f358df0%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719736000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGFFg_H6LVvsjCxk5PPfelU6iFlqA" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blood_is_thicker_than_water#cite_note-7" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank">[7]</a></span>. This usage of the term was common in the English-speaking world at least as early as the mid 1300s. Because English speakers around that time would have understood the word "blood" as referring to family, it is likely that the use of "blood" in the expression "blood is thicker than water" would also have been understood by English speakers referring to family.</span><br /><span style="font-size: xx-small;"><br /></span><span style="font-size: xx-small;">Although not specifically related to the expression "blood is thicker than water", H.C. Trumbull notes an interesting comparison of blood and milk in the Arab world:</span><br /><span style="font-size: xx-small;"><br /></span><br /><table class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-cquote" style="border-collapse: collapse;"><tbody><tr><td style="font-size: 13px; padding: 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">"</span></td><td style="font-size: 13px; padding: 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">We, in the West, are accustomed to say that "blood is thicker than water"&nbsp;; but the Arabs have the idea that blood is thicker than milk, than a mother's milk. With them, any two children nourished at the same breast are called "milk-brothers," or "sucking brothers"; and the tie between such is very strong. [..] But the Arabs hold that brothers in the covenant of blood are closer than brothers at a common breast; that those who have tasted each other's blood are in a surer covenant than those who have tasted the same milk together&nbsp;; that "blood-lickers," as the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3Deb40cf8d-3e47-4167-aa23-269d0798fb0d%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719736000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGxPxE_07KelKzrs9jR1q9YkuVVsA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blood_brother" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Blood brother">blood-brothers</a>&nbsp;are sometimes called, are more truly one than "milk-brothers," or "sucking brothers"; that, indeed, blood is thicker than milk, as well as thicker than water.<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-cite_ref-8" style="font-size: 6.75px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline;"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D924f7357-943f-4d25-9ab0-a1ade4f8f29f%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719736000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGJamhF1pBHQPSWDoE6Bym9ZbLZDA" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blood_is_thicker_than_water#cite_note-8" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank">[8]</a></span></span></td><td style="font-size: 13px; padding: 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">"</span></td></tr></tbody></table></div></div></div><div class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-separator" style="font-family: Lora, serif; font-size: 20px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">More recently,&nbsp;</span><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3De6971dfd-00ba-4676-abe0-a9a989924900%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719736000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGdMPEF2r4py93G4-xTcKp6NwdvqQ" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aldous_Huxley" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: x-small;" target="_blank" title="Aldous Huxley">Aldous Huxley</a><span style="font-size: xx-small;">'s&nbsp;</span><em style="font-size: x-small;">Ninth Philosopher's Song</em><span style="font-size: xx-small;">&nbsp;(1920) approached the proverb differently, stating, "Blood, as all men know, than water's thicker&nbsp;/ But water's wider, thank the Lord, than blood."</span><span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-cite_ref-9" style="font-size: 15px; The fish in the Nile will die, and the river will stink and the Egyptians will not be able to drink its water.<br /><div class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-templatequotecite" style="font-family: arial, sans-serif;"><cite>— Exodus 7:17–18</cite></div></blockquote></div></div><div class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-separator"><strong style="font-family: Lora, serif; font-size: 20px;'>), feminine&nbsp;</span><strong style="font-family: Lora, serif; font-size: 20px;">Naunet</strong><span style='font-family: "lora" , serif; font-size: 20px;'>&nbsp;(also&nbsp;</span><em style="font-family: Lora, serif; The name is paralleled with&nbsp;</span><em style="font-family: Lora, serif; font-size: 20px;">nen</em><span style='font-family: "lora" , serif; font-size: 20px;'>&nbsp;"inactivity" in a play of words in, "I raised them up from out of the watery mass [</span><em style="font-family: Lora, serif; font-size: 20px;">nu</em><span style='font-family: "lora" , serif; font-size: 20px;'>], out of inactivity [</span><em style="font-family: Lora, serif; font-size: 20px;">nen</em><span style='font-family: "lora" , serif; font-size: 20px;'>]". She shares the fruit with Adam, and as a result the first humans are expelled from the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3Df0887df4-aee8-4dd9-a479-e221ac3a93b0%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719744000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGg8eD_JZ5aGeuXqjVRPIpzt8202g" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Garden_of_Eden" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Garden of Eden">Garden of Eden</a>. Christian churches differ on how they view both Adam and Eve's disobedience to God (often called the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D177a5635-4ae5-49c0-bb3e-384dd49207bd%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719744000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFFbMK-CpytQeksYJAKboqsMRljYA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fall_of_man" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Fall of man">fall of man</a>), and to the consequences that those actions had on the rest of humanity. These were the only objects in the sky visible to ancient astronomers (who had no&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D7f56e8cd-8406-4fbe-ac2a-3314cb50c0a8%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719753000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEjYMxKy-Jrom5tsAMkDcJ35SM6Ig" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Telescope" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Fixed stars">fixed stars</a>.<br /><br />&nbsp;The seventh heaven, which borrows some concepts from its Jewish counterpart, is depicted as being composed of divine light incomprehensible to the mortal man.&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D06c0c85c-a16a-44b6-ad8b-182e049bdcea%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719753000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGEJVre2ZlFgjaZVU1srxPGJEemcA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abraham" style="background: transparent; Excalibur was associated with the&nbsp;<a class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-mw-redirect" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D1589fc73-b9cf-4a87-9927-66dd3430d604%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719754000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHHwV23AdU_Hez3_fx1VIYP-ePxJg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arthurian_legend" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Arthurian legend">Arthurian legend</a>&nbsp;very early. This event is the point at which the sun begins its regeneration; it is a moment of great significance, but also danger, as beyond it in hour 7 the adversary&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D59105369-13d8-46c7-9e06-00e6c59c2837%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719756000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFp-T_aG8DhPCGeFb-FuWcXdFaG_g" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Apep" rel="noopener" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Apep">Apep</a>&nbsp;(Apophis) lies in wait and has to be subdued by the magic of Isis, and the strength of&nbsp;<a class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-m_-1864275979709954742gmail-m_-5894527381479939783gmail-mw-redirect" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3Da8d72204-bd73-4928-9148-1302738e1486%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719756000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGvoeMtUNJ6f1jgHVf8FAFaniRbyg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Set_(mythology)" rel="noopener" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Set (mythology)">Set</a>&nbsp;assisted by&nbsp;<a class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-m_-1864275979709954742gmail-m_-5894527381479939783gmail-mw-redirect" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D47a267e4-af15-40f7-a8b5-9de1861c52ff%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719756000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFml95N5ZDnOG_cSQTncPLen_UNyg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serqet" rel="noopener" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Serqet">Serqet</a>. Once this has been done the sun god opens the doors of the tomb in hour 8 and then leaves the sandy island of&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D5ff27407-b6dd-4213-b934-22d393b87124%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719756000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHnEd5_FQJdfSMoEwntLqL-ZtB1xQ" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Seker" rel="noopener" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Seker">Sokar</a>&nbsp;by rowing vigorously back into the waters in hour 9. In hour 10 the regeneration process continues through immersion in the waters until in hour 11 the god's eyes (a symbol for his health and well being) are fully regenerated.<strong>&nbsp;In hour 12 he enters the east</strong>ern horizon ready to rise again as the new day's sun.<br /><br /></div><div></div><div><span style="font-size: xx-small;"><em><strong>Shadow of the Hegemon</strong></em>&nbsp;(2001) is the second novel in the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D1cbedad8-feb4-4e29-abbf-c2ae2b4dc16e%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719756000&amp;usg=AFQjCNG85WqEEe9ozxf8w-uNJtqT5qFZkg" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ender%27s_Game_(series)#Shadow_saga" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Ender's Game (series)"><em>Ender's Shadow</em>&nbsp;series</a>&nbsp;(often called the Bean Quartet) by&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D3eb2c9a7-d332-4ec7-b5a9-44f5b9ccda57%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719756000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFepRVxvfMd7aYABPmeQNO1Y62udQ" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Orson_Scott_Card" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Orson Scott Card">Orson Scott Card</a>. It is also the sixth novel in the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3Dc2f3106b-c30d-4c0d-81bd-a25cbc6aaac5%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719756000&amp;usg=AFQjCNG8n-P_-U4htUoZFoTuccHkvRCQXA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ender%27s_Game_(series)" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Ender's Game (series)"><em>Ender's Game</em>&nbsp;series</a>. Saul reluctantly agrees and offers his armor, which David declines, taking only his staff,&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D9f8863f1-9e34-463f-a0a3-b8e6d29db77e%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719758000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHYbykaoUQm0gW-NYfXRlc2qT46Wg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sling_(weapon)" style="background: transparent; font-size: 11px;">David and Goliath confront each other, Goliath with his armor and javelin, David with his staff and sling. "The Philistine cursed David by his gods", but David replies: "This day the L<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_-2943162030376724839m_4715356690998560955gmail-m_-7537480698924484776m_-278294240238056367gmail-m_-5546344077922119487gmail-m_3924190074418593144gmail-m_201252411975995256gmail-smallcaps">ORD</span>&nbsp;will deliver you into my hand, and I will strike you down; and I will give the dead bodies of the host of the Philistines this day to the birds of the air and to the wild beasts of the earth; that all the earth may know that there is a God in Israel, and that all this assembly may know that God saves not with sword and spear; for the battle is God's, and he will give you into our hand."<br /><br />David hurls a stone from his sling and hits Goliath in the center of his forehead, Goliath falls on his face to the ground, and David cuts off his head. The Philistines flee and are pursued by the Israelites "as far as Gath and the gates of&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3Db53974a5-410f-48c9-8ad3-782c7a9356e2%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719758000&amp;usg=AFQjCNE5V6V3PpXJLZp8D1kc7c6ybk28sQ" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ekron" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Ekron">Ekron</a>". David puts the armor of Goliath in his own tent and takes the head to&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3Dbee06ec7-65d6-4f8a-b117-706ba518c23c%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719758000&amp;usg=AFQjCNExnBPKvKP7eKhDhIckMsUZdf9NCQ" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jerusalem" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Jerusalem">Jerusalem</a>, and Saul sends&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D36a96d97-e8c2-42cb-8098-d9413ecf3e34%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719758000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGAwTqargdMfm6sDQ6YOvjRYk2p1g" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abner" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Abner">Abner</a>&nbsp;to bring the boy to him. The king asks whose son he is, and David answers, "I am the son of your servant&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D93cb8f9d-a0d0-4d97-a481-0a382e574177%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719758000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEp-5bOMfTGGUag_cLovwCLhcU-Uw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jesse" style="background: transparent; color: #25a186; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Jesse">Jesse</a>&nbsp;the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D682af421-72af-4b8b-bc90-9e1cb0011936%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719758000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGrgS81zTcCx-EvZAvXMdyeuXoABw" Most sources describe her as the daughter of&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://gmass.co/x/c?c%3D1387619%26l%3D1b65fc93-2644-41d1-871d-15881fe8e6b8%26r%3Ddd8bd842-6e53-4ecd-b8d2-cc32cd4edec1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719759000&amp;usg=AFQjCNG7M37sf9uLQFmtIG15fdofUDKJqQ" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Phorcys" style="background: transparent; font-size: 11px; text-align: justify; width: 300px;"><strong><br /></strong></div><div style="color: black; font-family: verdana, arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 11px; text-align: justify; width: 300px;"><strong>John Hancock&nbsp;</strong>(January 23, 1737 [<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Style_and_New_Style_dates&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719761000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHDKO8L__lSlvtddAaLv8ZALizJkw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Style_and_New_Style_dates" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Old Style and New Style dates">O.S.</a>&nbsp;January 12, 1736]&nbsp;–&nbsp;October 8, 1793) was an American merchant, statesman, and prominent&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Patriot_(American_Revolution)&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719761000&amp;usg=AFQjCNF0NjQYg0OhOStAMnxBjo5ETEYn2g" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Patriot_(American_Revolution)" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Patriot (American Revolution)">Patriot</a>&nbsp;of the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Revolution&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719761000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEL6gOrije1IlLKlqEJaR8mzVjycQ" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Revolution" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="American Revolution">American Revolution</a>. He served as&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/President_of_the_Continental_Congress&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719761000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFiyBO45Vs9K3Z84vPsSIj0enov3g" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/President_of_the_Continental_Congress" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="President of the Continental Congress">president</a>&nbsp;of the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Second_Continental_Congress&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719761000&amp;usg=AFQjCNH0vGYzwh_Pe8lK4yd8GdLIcPxmkw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Second_Continental_Congress" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Second Continental Congress">Second Continental Congress</a>&nbsp;and was the&nbsp;<a class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_540843752078009674gmail-m_-2147698511185508770gmail-mw-redirect" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_Governors_of_Massachusetts&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719761000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEhPoMVbjlmocefgjYOnX_maxBw1g" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_Governors_of_Massachusetts" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="List of Governors of Massachusetts">first and third</a>&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Governor_of_Massachusetts&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719761000&amp;usg=AFQjCNE5HsYWaaGWYM8DGnwD9UU6tOZKJw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Governor_of_Massachusetts" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Governor of Massachusetts">Governor</a>&nbsp;of the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Massachusetts&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719761000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGNd4XR3StW1PczDVIhwvYNzQg8Mw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Massachusetts" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Massachusetts">Commonwealth of Massachusetts</a>. He is remembered for his large and stylish signature on the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Declaration_of_Independence&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719761000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGiwoUfmD3mfSwYUv-3ISFhR2fjbA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Declaration_of_Independence" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="United States Declaration of Independence">United States Declaration of Independence</a>,<br /><br /></div><div style="color: black; font-family: verdana, arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 11px; text-align: justify; width: 300px;">Osiris is the mythological father of the god&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Horus&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719762000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHIhsm50UY5HDOMX_cJ0nB18mG4hg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Horus" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Horus">Horus</a>, whose conception is described in the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Osiris_myth&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719762000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHBq8M5cAlTL4daiQqFUonNYNESQQ" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Osiris_myth" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Osiris myth">Osiris myth</a>, a central myth in&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Egyptian_religion&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719762000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHSUbZSYMjF7oFsXx-Lc9wIvrTEMw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Egyptian_religion" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Ancient Egyptian religion">ancient Egyptian belief</a>. The myth described Osiris as having been killed by his brother Set, who wanted Osiris' throne. Isis joined the fragmented pieces of Osiris, but the only body part missing was the phallus. Isis fashioned a golden phallus, and briefly brought Osiris back to life by use of a spell that she learned from&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Geb&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719762000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEJNxdIZJ0ed1RNdIuXPWk9Sl6Irg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Geb" style="background: transparent; color: #970101; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Geb">her father</a>. This spell gave her time to become pregnant by Osiris before he again died. Isis later gave birth to Horus. As such, since Horus was born after Osiris' resurrection, Horus became thought of as a representation of new beginnings and the vanquisher of the evil Set.</div></center></div><div style="font-size: 20px;"><br /></div><div style="font-size: 20px;"><img alt="Image result" height="554" src="reqs/fromthemachine.org/irmax_files/ROBzu7AOodNDSMI4tDnIJIcJIGaSuhpG5m_ah9qt0Ud7HmaC1FxPi1MQmYbTtMMTl7i6fqx45V5bn6hNRGq6yUT7ePRbY69MQWYFKhXkIMd-UkABafpa0fi-PA=s0-d-e1-ft" style="border: 0px; height: auto; margin-right: 0px; max-width: 100%;" width="369" /></div><div style="text-align: center;"><center style="color: black; font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; text-align: justify; width: 300px;"><br /><span style="font-size: 20px;">Maybe it's funnier than "it looks."</span><br /><br /><div style="font-size: 11px;">In&nbsp;<a class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_540843752078009674gmail-m_-2147698511185508770external m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_540843752078009674gmail-m_-2147698511185508770gmail-text" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://www.mechon-mamre.org/p/pt/pt0117.htm%231&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719762000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGj5kq3A8w7ZNe6b_EFRpsqBTKUHQ" href="http://www.mechon-mamre.org/p/pt/pt0117.htm#1" rel="nofollow" style="background: transparent; color: #970101;" target="_blank">Genesis 17</a>&nbsp;when Abram was ninety-nine years old, God declared his new name: "Abraham"&nbsp;– "a father of many nations", and gave him the covenant of circumcision. God gave Sarai the new name "Sarah", and blessed her.<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_540843752078009674gmail-m_-2147698511185508770gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-m_-6182954198820330264gmail-m_521289457461777515m_1359743985997052155m_2062399313490225364m_7360525420591546646gmail-m_540843752078009674gmail-m_-2147698511185508770gmail-cite_ref-16" style="font-size: 8.25px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline;"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sarah%23cite_note-16&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719762000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGhlRikMfzubFmMOvu_5lk-sNpTcw" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sarah#cite_note-16" style="background: transparent; color: #970101;" target="_blank">[16]</a></span>&nbsp;Abraham was given assurance that Sarah would have a son. Not long afterwards, Abraham and Sarah were visited by three men. One of the visitors told Abraham that upon his return next year, Sarah would have a son. While at the tent entrance, Sarah overheard what was said, and she laughed to herself about the prospect of having a child at their ages. The visitor inquired of Abraham why Sarah laughed at the idea of bearing a child, for her age was as nothing to God. Sarah soon became pregnant and bore a son to Abraham, at the very time which had been spoken. The patriarch, then a hundred years old, named the child "<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719762000&amp;usg=AFQjCNG38DB_uwpPb0SH9W9-9H6pfD-87g" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac" style="background: transparent; style="font-size: 20px; text-align: center;"><center><div style="text-align: justify; width: 445px;"><div><span style="font-size: xx-small;">The&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grinch&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719766000&amp;usg=AFQjCNG2Jdee-vlvRXDTSUdDeOO5IWi44g" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grinch" style="color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Grinch">Grinch</a>&nbsp;is a bitter, grouchy, cave-dwelling creature with a heart "two sizes too small" who lives on snowy Mount Crumpit, a steep high mountain just north of the town of&nbsp;<b>Who</b>ville, home of the merry and warm-hearted&nbsp;<b>Who</b>s. His only companion is his unloved, but loyal dog,&nbsp;<span style='font-family: "arial black" , sans-serif;'>Max</span>. From his cave, the Grinch can hear the noisy Christmas festivities that take place in&nbsp;<b>Who</b>ville. Annoyed, he decides to stop Christmas from coming by stealing their presents, trees, and food for their Christmas feast. He crudely disguises himself as Santa Claus, and forces Max, disguised as a reindeer, to drag a sleigh to&nbsp;<b>Who</b>ville. Once there, the Grinch slides down the chimney and steals all of the&nbsp;<b>Who</b>s' Christmas presents, the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christmas_tree&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719766000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHBrHkQwIEbzwxSZsBr7F8i8Xa9qw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christmas_tree" style="color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Christmas tree">Christmas tree</a>, and the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yule_log&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719766000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEUanaHajIo16GRoa16pIYbLbuPwg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yule_log" style="color: #25a186;" target="_blank" title="Yule log">log</a>&nbsp;for their fire. He is briefly interrupted in his burglary by Cindy Lou, a little Who girl, but concocts a crafty lie to effect his escape from her home.</span></div><div><br /></div></div></center></div><div width: 445px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;"><br /></span></div><div style="text-align: justify; width: 445px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;"><b style="font-family: sans-serif; text-align: start;">Caleb</b><span style="font-family: sans-serif; text-align: start;">, sometimes transliterated as&nbsp;</span><b style="font-family: sans-serif; text-align: start;">Kaleb</b><span style="font-family: sans-serif; text-align: start;">&nbsp;(</span><span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-script-hebrew" dir="rtl" style='font-family: "alef" , "sbl biblit" , "sbl hebrew" , "david clm" , "frenk ruehl clm" , "hadasim clm" , "cardo" , "shofar" , "david" , "ezra sil" , "ezra sil sr" , "noto sans hebrew" , "freeserif" , "times new roman" , "freesans" , "arial"; text-align: start;">;&nbsp;</span><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tiberian_vocalization&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719767000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGppvMHZd55sGFt9xJX3e9Hkrj7oQ" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tiberian_vocalization" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Hebrew Academy">Hebrew Academy</a><span style="font-family: sans-serif; text-align: start;">: Kalev), is a figure who appears in the&nbsp;</span><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_Bible&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719767000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHQQyTrPm-xHwbz8xuzjFrgaBe63g" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_Bible" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Hebrew Bible">Hebrew Bible</a><span style="font-family: sans-serif; text-align: start;">&nbsp;as a representative of the&nbsp;</span><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tribe_of_Judah&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719767000&amp;usg=AFQjCNG3DGBRp-Z38qhckERZnD8mHNhguA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tribe_of_Judah" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Tribe of Judah">Tribe of Judah</a><span style="font-family: sans-serif; text-align: start;">&nbsp;during the&nbsp;</span><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Israelites&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719767000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGXg5RGsIfrZIaPAf9Ucech5jzPUA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Israelites" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="The Exodus">journey</a><span style="font-family: sans-serif; text-align: start;">&nbsp;to the&nbsp;</span><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Promised_Land&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719767000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGPgfewfOQgH5mQWwkImNQwt4Q_Lg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Promised_Land" style="background-image: none; width: 445px;"><div style="font-family: sans-serif; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.5em 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">According to the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jewish_Encyclopedia&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719767000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHCvQgr8tQUzbf3vcKp5XU1K8063g" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jewish_Encyclopedia" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Jewish Encyclopedia">Jewish Encyclopedia</a>, "since 'Caleb' signifies dog, it has been thought that the dog was the totem of [Caleb's] clan".<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-cite_ref-1" style="font-size: 6.75px; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank">[1]</a></span>&nbsp;The New American Standard Exhaustive Concordance states that the name&nbsp;<i>Kaleb</i>&nbsp;(Caleb) is related to the word for "dog" (<i>keleb</i>).<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-cite_ref-2" style="font-size: 6.75px; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank">[2]</a></span>&nbsp;It should be noted that the Bible was written down centuries before&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_diacritics&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719767000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHlGfIi6W6EnldYZIzoRjN8-tjKGg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_diacritics" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Hebrew diacritics">Hebrew diacritics</a>&nbsp;were introduced, and there is no certain knowledge of how the name was pronounced when the biblical text was written.</span></div><div style="font-family: sans-serif; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.5em 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">In Hebrew, the name is pronounced&nbsp;<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-nowrap" style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-IPA m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-nopopups m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-noexcerpt"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA/English&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719767000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFPlyJQ8s51-aDODCJ-dYfGKni8Ng" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA/English" style="background-image: none; the modern English pronunciation&nbsp;<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-nowrap" style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-IPA m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-nopopups m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-noexcerpt"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA/English&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719767000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFPlyJQ8s51-aDODCJ-dYfGKni8Ng" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA/English" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Jephunneh">Jephunneh</a>&nbsp;(Numbers 13:6) is not to be confused with Caleb, great-grandson of&nbsp;<a class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-mw-redirect" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Judah_(biblical_person)&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHF7TUM8mnuydXIZYa-DUFJIsVQ-A" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Judah_(biblical_person)" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Judah (biblical person)">Judah</a>&nbsp;through&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tamar_(Genesis)&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGVHct0fSC3MUXjBpSjTPfbfTJf_g" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tamar_(Genesis)" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Tamar (Genesis)">Tamar</a>&nbsp;(1 Chronicles 2:3-9). This other Caleb was the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb_(son_of_Hezron)&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGlyupxq8Jhm9ROJWJpCG0DLOE0Qg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb_(son_of_Hezron)" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Caleb (son of Hezron)">son of Hezron</a>, and his wife was Azubah (I Chronicles 2:18,19).</span></div><div style="font-family: sans-serif; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.5em 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">According to Numbers 13, Caleb, the son of Jephunneh, was one of&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Twelve_Spies&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNE9h5Oo9X6ooJ9BZ_Ep_jHs52JoIw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Twelve_Spies" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="The Twelve Spies">the twelve spies</a>&nbsp;sent by&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moses&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNF7AUdAMRn8fbhvFEHYq0ZGus_9oA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moses" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Moses">Moses</a>&nbsp;into Canaan. Their task, over a period of 40 days,<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-cite_ref-3" style="font-size: 6.75px; line-height: 1; unicode-bidi: isolate; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: nowrap;"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb%23cite_note-3&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHCeyxNVIRD5a01yS2JXbIL4XZwWA" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb#cite_note-3" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank">[3]</a></span>&nbsp;was to explore the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Negev&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHLD9hhGiYf6_xRP7nVP0E-0oT6yw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Negev" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Negev">Negev</a>&nbsp;and surrounding area, and to make an assessment of the geographical features of the land, the strength and numbers of the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Population&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNECVypjNDh2ieh1ZQ86LXkCo2zbLA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Population" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Population">population</a>, the&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Agriculture&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGOtOqBb3RpVjq-g3Qg_uOfzbA_0w" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Agriculture" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Agriculture">agricultural</a>&nbsp;potential and actual performance of the land, settlement patterns (whether their&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/City&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGSY06v7vmh7fAEvd2nRBaW9yMkFA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/City" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="City">cities</a>&nbsp;were like camps or strongholds), and&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Forestry&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFqCu80BCvALT_9KfgNGJiFnmFamA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Forestry" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Forestry">forestry</a>&nbsp;conditions. Moses also asked them to be courageous and to return with samples of local produce.<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-cite_ref-4" style="font-size: 6.75px; line-height: 1; unicode-bidi: isolate; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: nowrap;"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb%23cite_note-4&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHJ-eJ1PaTX6KnqOuxcb_DQKwxBPg" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb#cite_note-4" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank">[4]</a></span></span></div><div style="font-family: sans-serif; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.5em 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">In the Numbers 13 listing of the heads of each tribe, verse 6 reads "Of the tribe of Judah, Caleb the son of Jephunneh." Caleb's report balanced the appeal of the land and its fruits with the challenge of making a conquest.</span></div><div style="font-family: sans-serif; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.5em 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">Verse 30 of chapter 13 reads "And Caleb stilled the people toward Moses, and said: 'We should go up at once, and possess it; for we are well able to overcome it.'"<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-cite_ref-5" style="font-size: 6.75px; line-height: 1; unicode-bidi: isolate; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: nowrap;"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb%23cite_note-5&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFOu5XSVqwEHaNHhoD7KB5XUvDjtg" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb#cite_note-5" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank">[5]</a></span>&nbsp;Caleb and&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joshua&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNG0TVw7xUGu7dCA9tVeub-alknTlw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joshua" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Joshua">Joshua</a>&nbsp;said the people should trust God and go into the land; the other ten spies, being fearful and rebellious, argued that conquering the land was impossible.</span></div><div><div style="font-family: sans-serif; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.5em 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">Caleb the spy is the son of Jephunneh. Jephunneh is called a&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenizzite&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFdXQDc57cgm-tGnR2ChffgBR6i9g" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenizzite" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Kenizzite">Kenizzite</a>&nbsp;(Numbers 32:12, Joshua 14:6,14). The Kenizzites are listed (Genesis 15:19) as one of the nations who lived in the land of Canaan, at the time that God covenanted with Abram (Abraham) to give that land to his descendants forever (Genesis 17:8). However, Caleb is mentioned alongside the descendants of Judah recorded in 1 Chronicles 4: "And the sons of Caleb the son of Jephunneh: Iru, Elah, and Naam; and the sons of Elah: Kenaz" (1 Chronicles 4:15).<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-cite_ref-6" style="font-size: 6.75px; line-height: 1; unicode-bidi: isolate; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: nowrap;"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb%23cite_note-6&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFmcHmh1uyfaM96G5Sn0sI32IuJzg" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb#cite_note-6" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank">[6]</a></span>&nbsp;Numbers 13:6, likewise, lists Caleb as a tribal leader in Judah.</span></div><div style="font-family: sans-serif; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.5em 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">The Kenizzites are generally considered an Edomite clan (see Genesis 36:40-43).<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-cite_ref-FreedmanMyers2000_7-0" style="font-size: 6.75px; line-height: 1; unicode-bidi: isolate; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: nowrap;"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb%23cite_note-FreedmanMyers2000-7&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHFsadWIp2rMba0uutbMCGrJwWnwg" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb#cite_note-FreedmanMyers2000-7" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank">[7]</a></span></span></div><div style="font-family: sans-serif; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.5em 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;"><b>Kaleb</b>&nbsp;(c. 520) is perhaps the best-documented, if not best-known, King of&nbsp;<a class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-mw-redirect" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kingdom_of_Axum&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGDGsuHWLikQhg1eL8Nt_cbATpbXg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kingdom_of_Axum" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Kingdom of Axum">Axum</a>&nbsp;situated in modern-day&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eritrea&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGD_v3Rx622ISH4weP0krkESlcBRA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eritrea" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Eritrea">Eritrea</a>&nbsp;and North&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ethiopia&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGOxYtZJxh08XdcsqL76l1QmY2ppg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ethiopia" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a>.</span></div><div style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0.5em 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;"><a class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-mw-redirect" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Procopius_of_Caesarea&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFb2Z2AEdQLyS0VxVe66ZlQb3eRXA" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Procopius_of_Caesarea" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Procopius of Caesarea">Procopius of Caesarea</a><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">&nbsp;calls him "</span><span style='font-family: "arial black" , sans-serif;'>Hellestheaeus</span><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">", a variant of his throne name&nbsp;</span><b style="font-family: sans-serif;">Ella Atsbeha</b><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">&nbsp;or&nbsp;</span><b style="font-family: sans-serif;">Ella Asbeha</b><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">&nbsp;(</span><i style="font-family: sans-serif;">Histories</i><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">, 1.20). Variants of his name are Hellesthaeus, Ellestheaeus, Eleshaah, Ella Atsbeha, Ellesboas, and Elesboam, all from the Greek Ελεσβόάς, for "The one who brought about the morning" or "The one who collected tribute."</span></span></div><div style="font-family: sans-serif; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.5em 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">At Aksum, in inscription RIE 191, his name is rendered in unvocalized Gə'əz as KLB 'L 'ṢBḤ WLD TZN (Kaleb ʾElla ʾAṣbeḥa son of Tazena). In vocalized Gə'əz, it is ካሌብ እለ አጽብሐ (Kaleb ʾƎllä ʾAṣbəḥa).</span></div><div style="font-family: sans-serif; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.5em 0px;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">Kaleb, a name derived from the Biblical character&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNF6S2CbnwtMdPXDhf31-P87M56C6w" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caleb" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Caleb">Caleb</a>, is his given biblical name; ʾOn both his coins and inscriptions he left at&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Axum&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHb6-TgnrUUoE0vg4C85VHlOEjN-Q" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Axum" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Axum">Axum</a>, as well as Ethiopian hagiographical sources and king lists, he refers to himself as the son of Tazena.<span class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-reference" id="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-cite_ref-7" style="font-size: 6.75px; line-height: 1; unicode-bidi: isolate; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: nowrap;"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kaleb_of_Axum%23cite_note-7&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNF_Q4REjUdCAWBGaNPxM9UEuHTRqA" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kaleb_of_Axum#cite_note-7" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank">[6]</a></span>&nbsp;He may be the "Atsbeha" or "Asbeha" of the Ethiopian legends of&nbsp;<a class="m_-2406931458228765498m_7062753601417727326gmail-m_258112447631369337m_2341308960067590409m_4521999671932699583gmail-new" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title%3DAbreha_and_Asbeha%26action%3Dedit%26redlink%3D1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHOPMN8kfHG1WHG0CrjXAci9hK1WQ" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abreha_and_Asbeha" style="background-image: none; color: #a55858; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Abreha and Asbeha (page does not exist)">Abreha and Asbeha</a>, the other possibility being&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ezana_of_Axum&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNH8tVye3bHX7nk_9tXlsDUG34H9vw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ezana_of_Axum" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Ezana of Axum">Ezana's</a>&nbsp;brother&nbsp;<a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saizana&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGiT7h4ZaTVqHTj3tWcIJFMwMyLsg" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saizana" style="background-image: none; color: #0b0080; font-family: arial, sans-serif;" target="_blank" title="Saizana">Saizana</a>.</span></div></div></div></center></div></div></center></div></div></div></div></div></div></center></div><div style="color: #292929; font-family: lora, serif; font-size: 20px; text-align: center;"><br /></div><div style="color: #292929; font-family: lora, serif; font-size: 20px; text-align: center;"><a data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://threetag.reallyhim.com&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1505066719768000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGbEzII34xSf9TZmMoEdsOjBTuWAg" href="./THREETAG.html" style="color: #25a186;
